</th>
<td>These 7 <i>words</i> belong to a selection of 20 Haydn string quartets.

<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>Köhler's arrangement of Haydn's '7 Worte' is based on the orchestral or choral version, as is made clear by A.Herring whose pencilled annotations do not come out well when scanned. Thus, we have a footnote for n°4 p.11, referring to the last stave but one, 4th measure which is marked with a (2)&#160;: "Qtt. (=Quartet) DC. with an added bar/if played with Qtt. the strings omit added bar (1) and proceed to (2)". On page 12 the closing measure is annotated thus&#160;: "In Qtt. the strings finish here &amp; omit next page (not int Qtt.)". A similar remark is attached to n°5 p.15 stave 4, measure 3&#160;: "Qtt. has D.C." and on page 20, end of stave 1&#160;: "Qtt. has DC"
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Die Worte des Erlösers am Kreuze
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Die sieben letzten Worte unseres Erlösers am Kreuze
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Haydn,_Joseph" title="Category:Haydn, Joseph">Haydn, Joseph</a>
</td></tr>

</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJH 610
</td></tr>

<ol><li>Introduzione. Adagio

</li><li>Sonata 2: Grave e cantabile
</li><li>Sonata 3: Grave
</li><li>Sonata 4: Largo
</li><li>Sonata 6: Adagio
</li><li>Sonata 6: Lento
</li><li>Sonata 7: Largo 
</li><li> Il Terremoto. Presto e con tutta la forza
</li></ol>
</td></tr>

<th>Piece Style

<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Orchestra:</i> 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 bassoons, 4 horns, 2 trumpets, timpani, strings
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Related Works
</th>
<td>For the chorus and orchestra setting, see <i><a href="/wiki/Die_Worte_des_Erl%C3%B6sers_am_Kreuze,_Hob.XX:2_(Haydn,_Joseph)" title="Die Worte des Erlösers am Kreuze, Hob.XX:2 (Haydn, Joseph)">Die Worte des Erlösers am Kreuze, Hob.XX:2</a></i>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://earsense.org/chamberbase/works/detail/?pkey=8503">Earsense page</a></span> (Hob.XX/1B)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>The work was composed for orchestra in 1785 and arrangements were made for string quartet (as Hob.XX/1B) and piano (as Hob.XX/1C) in time for publication of all three instrumental settings by Artaria in 1787. The chorus and orchestra setting came a decade later in 1796 and was published in 1801 by Breitkopf und Härtel. <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Special:WikiForum&amp;thread=15976"><i>More about the arrangements</i></a></span>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
